############################################################################
#	Garrison roles
############################################################################

garrison_role = {
	roles = { garrison }
	upgrade_prio = {
		factor = 1

		#ROLE PRIORITY
		modifier = { #make a front line design first
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = infantry_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = infantry } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = marine_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = marine } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = mountaineer } }
			}
		}
		modifier = { #make an at/armor design first if it has the tech for it
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marm_army_focus OR = { has_tech = basic_medium_tank has_tech = improved_medium_tank has_tech = advanced_medium_tank } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = armor } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = harm_army_focus OR = { has_tech = basic_heavy_tank has_tech = improved_heavy_tank has_tech = advanced_heavy_tank } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = heavy_armor } }

				AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_AT has_tech = interwar_antitank NOT = { ai_has_role_template = at_infantry } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_MTD OR = { has_tech = basic_medium_td has_tech = improved_medium_td has_tech = advanced_medium_td } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = at_infantry } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_HTD OR = { has_tech = basic_heavy_td has_tech = improved_heavy_td has_tech = advanced_heavy_td } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = at_infantry } }
			}
		}

		#EVENT TEMPLATE FIX
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = infantry_army_focus NOT = { has_country_flag = infantry_template } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = marine_army_focus NOT = { has_country_flag = marine_template } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_army_focus NOT = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_template } }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			armor_tech_focus = yes
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marm_army_focus NOT = { has_country_flag = marm_template } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = harm_army_focus NOT = { has_country_flag = harm_template } }
			}
		}

		#FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = garrison_rotation } }
	}
	match_to_count = 0.6
	#available_for = {}
	#blocked_for = {}

	#include the starting templates in the role so that they can be upgraded
	early_garrison_template = {
		upgrade_prio = {
			factor = 0
		}
		production_prio = {
			factor = 0.01
		}

		#can_upgrade_in_field = {}

		#replace_at_match =
		#replace_with =
		#target_min_match =

		reinforce_prio = 0
		#custom_icon = 6

		#TEMPLATE
		target_width = 6
		width_weight = 1
		column_swap_factor = 0.5

		target_template = {
			weight = 1
			match_value = 1000

			regiments = {
				infantry = 3
			}

			support = {
				engineer = 1
			}
		}

		allowed_types = {
			#REGIMENTS
			infantry

			#SUPPORT
			engineer
			artillery
		}

		stat_weights = {
			0.0 #-- default_morale
			10.0 #-- defense
			0.0 #-- breakthrough
			0.0 #-- hardness
			0.0 #-- soft_attack
			0.0 #-- hard_attack
			0.0 #-- recon
			0.0 #-- entrenchment
			0.0 #-- initiative
			0.0 #-- casualty_trickleback
			-0.0 #-- supply_consumption_factor
			-0.0 #-- supply_consumption
			0.0 #-- suppression
			0.0 #-- suppression_factor
			0.0 #-- experience_loss_factor
			#-- Air Values
			0.0 #-- air_attack
			#-- Common Values
			0.0 #-- max_organisation
			0.0 #-- max_strength
			0.0 #-- build_cost_ic
			0.0 #-- maximum_speed
			0.0 #-- armor_value
			0.0 #-- ap_attack
			0.0 #-- reliability
			0.0 #-- reliability_factor
			0.0 #-- weight
        }
	}

	###################
	garrison_template = {
		upgrade_prio = {
			factor = 1
		}
		production_prio = {
			factor = 1
		}

		#can_upgrade_in_field = {}

		#replace_at_match =
		#replace_with =
		#target_min_match =

		reinforce_prio = 0
		custom_icon = 6

		#TEMPLATE
		target_width = 12
		width_weight = 1
		column_swap_factor = 0.5

		target_template = {
			weight = 1
			match_value = 1000

			regiments = {
				infantry = 6
			}

			support = {
				engineer = 1
				artillery = 1
			}
		}

		allowed_types = {
			#REGIMENTS
			infantry

			#SUPPORT
			engineer
			artillery
		}

		stat_weights = {
			0.0 #-- default_morale
			10.0 #-- defense
			0.0 #-- breakthrough
			0.0 #-- hardness
			0.0 #-- soft_attack
			0.0 #-- hard_attack
			0.0 #-- recon
			0.0 #-- entrenchment
			0.0 #-- initiative
			0.0 #-- casualty_trickleback
			-0.0 #-- supply_consumption_factor
			-0.0 #-- supply_consumption
			0.0 #-- suppression
			0.0 #-- suppression_factor
			0.0 #-- experience_loss_factor
			#-- Air Values
			0.0 #-- air_attack
			#-- Common Values
			0.0 #-- max_organisation
			0.0 #-- max_strength
			0.0 #-- build_cost_ic
			0.0 #-- maximum_speed
			0.0 #-- armor_value
			0.0 #-- ap_attack
			0.0 #-- reliability
			0.0 #-- reliability_factor
			0.0 #-- weight
        }
	}
}

############################################################################
#	Infantry roles

infantry_role = {
	roles = { infantry }
	upgrade_prio = {
		factor = 1

		#ARMY FOCUS WEIGHT
		#modifier = { factor = 10 has_country_flag = infantry_army_focus }

		#ARMY FOCUS REQ. #every country should create an improved infantry design regardless
		#modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = infantry_army_focus has_country_flag = infantry_attachment_1 has_country_flag = infantry_attachment_2 } }

		#ROLE PRIORITY
		modifier = { #make a front line design first
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marine_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = marine } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = mountaineer } }
			}
		}
		modifier = { #countries with a high priority on armor make armor designs before special force designs
			factor = 0
			armor_tech_focus = yes
			OR = { has_country_flag = infantry_attachment_1 has_country_flag = infantry_attachment_2 }
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marm_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = armor } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = harm_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = heavy_armor } }
			}
		}

		#EVENT TEMPLATE FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = infantry_template } }

		#FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = infantry_rotation } }
	}
	match_to_count = 0.85
	#available_for = {}
	#blocked_for = {}

	#include the starting templates in the role so that they can be upgraded
	early_infantry_template = {
		upgrade_prio = {

			weight = 1
			match_value = 1000

				infantry = 9
			}

			support = {
				engineer = 1
			}

			#REGIMENTS
			infantry
			artillery_brigade

			engineer
			recon
			artillery

			0.0 #-- default_morale

	######################################################## design A (inf+art)

	################### normal design
	sf_infantry_template_A_regular_RART = {
		upgrade_prio = {
			factor = 3

			#DESIGN REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = infantry_design_A } }

			#DATE REQ.
			#modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { date > 1938.1.1 } }

			#DOCTRINE REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = sf_doctrine } }

			#TECH REQ.
			#modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_tech = rocket_artillery } }

			#ARMY FOCUS REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 OR = { has_country_flag = infantry_attachment_1 has_country_flag = infantry_attachment_2 } }

			#ADVISOR REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 prefer_artillery_design = yes }
		}
		production_prio = {
			factor = 3

			#DESIGN REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = infantry_design_A } }

			#DATE REQ.
			#modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { date > 1938.1.1 } }

			#DOCTRINE REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = sf_doctrine } }

			#modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_tech = rocket_artillery } }

			#ADVISOR REQ.
			modifier = { factor = 0 prefer_artillery_design = yes }
		}

		#can_upgrade_in_field = {}

		#replace_at_match =
		#replace_with =
		#target_min_match =

		#TEMPLATE

		width_weight = 1
		column_swap_factor = 0.5

		target_template = {
			weight = 1
			match_value = 1000

			regiments = {
				infantry = 9
				artillery_brigade = 3
			}

			support = {
				engineer = 1
				artillery = 1
				recon = 1

				rocket_artillery = 1
			}
		}

		}

marine_role = {
	roles = { marine }
	upgrade_prio = {
		factor = 1

		#ARMY FOCUS WEIGHT
		#modifier = { factor = 10 has_country_flag = marine_army_focus }

		#ARMY FOCUS REQ.
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = marine_army_focus has_country_flag = marine_attachment_1 has_country_flag = marine_attachment_2 } }

		#ROLE PRIORITY
		modifier = { #make a front line design first
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marine_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = marine } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = mountaineer } }
			}
		}
		modifier = { #countries with a high priority on armor make armor designs before special force designs
			factor = 0
			armor_tech_focus = yes
			OR = { has_country_flag = marine_attachment_1 has_country_flag = marine_attachment_2 }
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marm_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = armor } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = harm_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = heavy_armor } }
			}
		}

mountaineer_role = {
	roles = { mountaineer }
	upgrade_prio = {
		factor = 1

		#ARMY FOCUS WEIGHT
		#modifier = { factor = 10 has_country_flag = mountaineer_army_focus }

		#ARMY FOCUS REQ.
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_army_focus has_country_flag = mountaineer_attachment_1 has_country_flag = mountaineer_attachment_2 } }

		#ROLE PRIORITY
		modifier = { #make a front line design first
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marine_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = marine } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = mountaineer } }
			}
		}
		modifier = { #countries with a high priority on armor make armor designs before special force designs
			factor = 0
			armor_tech_focus = yes
			OR = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_attachment_1 has_country_flag = mountaineer_attachment_2 }
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marm_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = armor } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = harm_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = heavy_armor } }
			}
		}

		#EVENT TEMPLATE FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_template } }

		#FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_rotation } }
	}
	match_to_count = 0.85

############################################################################
#	Anti-tank roles
############################################################################

at_infantry_role = {
	roles = { at_infantry }
	upgrade_prio = {
		factor = 1

		#ARMY FOCUS WEIGHT
		#modifier = { factor = 100 has_country_flag = AT_army_focus }

		#ROLE PRIORITY
		modifier = { #make a front line design first
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = infantry_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = infantry } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = marine_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = marine } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = mountaineer } }
			}
		}
		modifier = { #countries with an armor focus make make armor designs first
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marm_army_focus OR = { has_tech = basic_medium_tank has_tech = improved_medium_tank has_tech = advanced_medium_tank } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = armor } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = harm_army_focus OR = { has_tech = basic_heavy_tank has_tech = improved_heavy_tank has_tech = advanced_heavy_tank } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = heavy_armor } }
			}
		}

		#TECH REQ.
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_AT NOT = { has_tech = interwar_antitank } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_MTD NOT = { has_tech = basic_medium_td has_tech = improved_medium_td has_tech = advanced_medium_td } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_HTD NOT = { has_tech = basic_heavy_td has_tech = improved_medium_td has_tech = advanced_medium_td } }
			}
		}

		#EVENT TEMPLATE FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = at_template } }

		#FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = at_rotation } }
	}
	match_to_count = 0.8
	#available_for = {}
	#blocked_for = {}

light_armor_role = {
	roles = { light_armor }
	upgrade_prio = {
		factor = 1

		#ROLE PRIORITY
		modifier = { #make a front line design first
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = infantry_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = infantry } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = marine_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = marine } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = mountaineer } }
			}
		}
		modifier = { #make an armor design first
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marm_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = armor } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = harm_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = heavy_armor } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = AT_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = at_infantry } }
			}
		}

		#TECH REQ.
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_tech = basic_light_tank } }

		#FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = larm_rotation } }
	}
	match_to_count = 0.45
	#available_for = {}
	#blocked_for = {}

	###################
	light_armor_template_A = {
		upgrade_prio = {
			factor = 1
		}
		production_prio = {
			factor = 1
		}

		#can_upgrade_in_field = {}

		#replace_at_match =
		#replace_with =
		#target_min_match =

		reinforce_prio = 1
		#custom_icon =

		#TEMPLATE
		target_width = 12
		width_weight = 1
		column_swap_factor = 0.5

		target_template = {
			weight = 1
			match_value = 1000

			regiments = {
				light_armor = 2
				motorized = 4

			support = {
				engineer = 1

			}
		}

			#REGIMENTS

			motorized

			#SUPPORT
			engineer
			recon
		}

		stat_weights = {
			0.0 #-- default_morale

			0.0 #-- breakthrough
			0.0 #-- hardness
			10.0 #-- soft_attack
			0.0 #-- hard_attack

			0.0 #-- suppression
			0.0 #-- suppression_factor
			0.0 #-- experience_loss_factor

		modifier = { factor = 0 date < 1946.1.1 NOT = { has_country_flag = harm_army_focus has_country_flag = harm_attachment } }

		#OTHER
		modifier = { factor = 0 has_country_flag = harm_attachment date < 1942.1.1 } #don't make a secondary armor role template until late game

		#TECH REQ.
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_tech = basic_heavy_tank has_tech = improved_heavy_tank has_tech = advanced_heavy_tank } }

############################################################################
#	Motorized roles
############################################################################

motorized_role = {
	roles = { motorized }
	upgrade_prio = {
		factor = 1

		#ARMY FOCUS REQ.
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = mot_attachment } }

		#ROLE PRIORITY
		modifier = { #make a front line design first
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = infantry_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = infantry } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = marine_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = marine } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = mountaineer_army_focus NOT = { ai_has_role_template = mountaineer } }
			}
		}
		modifier = { #make an at/armor design first if it has the tech for it
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = marm_army_focus OR = { has_tech = basic_medium_tank has_tech = improved_medium_tank has_tech = advanced_medium_tank } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = armor } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = harm_army_focus OR = { has_tech = basic_heavy_tank has_tech = improved_heavy_tank has_tech = advanced_heavy_tank } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = heavy_armor } }

				AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_AT has_tech = interwar_antitank NOT = { ai_has_role_template = at_infantry } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_MTD OR = { has_tech = basic_medium_td has_tech = improved_medium_td has_tech = advanced_medium_td } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = at_infantry } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = at_design_HTD OR = { has_tech = basic_heavy_td has_tech = improved_heavy_td has_tech = advanced_heavy_td } NOT = { ai_has_role_template = at_infantry } }
			}
		}

		#TECH REQ.
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = { has_country_flag = mot_design_A NOT = { has_tech = basic_medium_art has_tech = improved_medium_art has_tech = advanced_medium_art } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = mot_design_B NOT = { has_tech = motorized_rocket_unit } }
				AND = { has_country_flag = mot_design_C NOT = { has_tech = basic_light_art has_tech = improved_light_art has_tech = advanced_light_art } }
			}
		}

		#EVENT TEMPLATE FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = mot_template } }

		#FIX
		modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_flag = mot_rotation } }
	}
	match_to_count = 0.8
	#available_for = {}
	#blocked_for = {}
